***старина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старина</a> (5870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старина́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stariná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старины́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>стари́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>стари́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>olden time, olden days, antiquity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старину́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v starinú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in olden times, formerly, in the old days</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тряхнуть.html>тряхну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старино́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trjaxnútʹ starinój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to revive a bit of the past, to go back to the good old days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>antiquities, antique</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">starínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старина́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stariná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старины́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>стари́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>стари́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> address</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> old man, old boy, old chap, old fellow</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a> (2217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stariná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starínnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>antique, ancient, olden, age-old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>starínnaja</b> mébelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>antique</b> furniture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>starínnyj</b> zámok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ancient</b> castle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нной</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>starínnoj</b> žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the <b>olden</b> days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>old <span class="use-with-mention">e.g. of relationships</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">my s nim <b>starínnyje</b> prijáteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he and I are <b>old</b> friends</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старость.html>ста́рость</a> (3057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starostь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ostь</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старость.html>ста́рость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stárostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старость.html>ста́рости</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>old age
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:старость.html>ста́рость</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stárostʹ</b> — ne rádostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">old age, boy, is no joy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dilapidation, decrepitude</li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-sense-notice-ru-"></span>Can we verify<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_verification/Non-Englishamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-sense/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5B%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C%23rfv-sense-notice-ru-%7c%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the elderly</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовать.html>стартова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">startovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

***стартовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a> (14340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старт.html>старт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">start</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stártovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> starting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovyj</b> pistolét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starting/starter's pistol</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>launching

***старший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a> (615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáršij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>elder, older, senior</li>
<li>eldest, oldest</li>
<li>higher, highest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> first (lieutenant)</li>
<li>senior (suffix used for names of elders)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáršij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́ршего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́ршие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рших</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foreman</li>
<li>chief, man in charge</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáršij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-iná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старшина.html>старшина́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">staršiná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старшина.html>старшины́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старшина.html>старшины́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старшина.html>старши́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sergeant major <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">military rank</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> prerevolutionary  Russia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foreman</li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:первенство.html>пе́рвенство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возраст.html>возрасту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́нию</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п.) <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>


</ol>
</body>

***старый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a> (185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">старъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)старе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>old</li>
<li>ancient, antique</li>
<li>olden</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The end-stressed short neuter form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>старо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staró</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used with the meaning "long-known" (of news, information, etc.), and in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>старо́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éto <b>staró</b> kak mir</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it's as <b>old</b> as the world</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; otherwise, the stem-stressed form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́ро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is preferred.</li></ul>
<p><i>Comparatives (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше and (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)старе́е:</i>
</p>
<ul><li>The comparative forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are used for comparing age or rank, e.g.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a> ста́рше <a href = vnd.unilang:девочка.html>де́вочки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Málʹčik stárše dévočki na dva góda.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The boy is older than the girl by two years</span></div>. The forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">старе́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staréje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">постаре́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postaréje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are used when both objects of comparison are "old", e.g.</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>стари́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>стано́вится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> старе́е <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> старе́е.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Starík stanóvitsja vsjó staréje i staréje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The old man is getting older and older.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Some sources claim that <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are only comparatives of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáršij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">elder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is itself originally an adjectival comparative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">исстари</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">isstari</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***стаскивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a> (12306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стаск-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stask-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáskivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag off, to drag down, to pull off, to pull down</li>
<li>to drag into, to pull into</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pull off</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снимать.html>снима́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стягивать.html>стя́гивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pull into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сводить.html>своди́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затягивать.html>затя́гивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затаскивать.html>зата́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:статистика.html>стати́стик</a> (9721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статистика.html>стати́стик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">statístik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
